document.getElementById('context-menu');\n379\t        if (!menu) return;\n380\t\n381\t        const container = menu.querySelector('.context-container');\n382\t        const viewportWidth = window.innerWidth;\n383\t        const viewportHeight = window.innerHeight;\n384\t\n385\t        // Get container dimensions\n386\t        const rect = container.getBoundingClientRect();\n387\t        const width = rect.width || 300;\n388\t        const height = rect.height || 400;\n389\t\n390\t        // Calculate position (keep within viewport)\n391\t        let left = x + 10;\n392\t        let top = y + 10;\n393\t\n394\t        // Adjust if off-screen\n395\t        if (left + width > viewportWidth) {\n396\t            left = x - width - 10;\n397\t        }\n398\t\n399\t        if (top + height > viewportHeight) {\n400\t            top = y - height - 10;\n401\t        }\n402\t\n403\t        // Ensure minimum margins\n404\t        left = Math.max(10, Math.min(left, viewportWidth - width - 10));\n405\t        top = Math.max(10, Math.min(top, viewportHeight - height - 10));\n406\t\n407\t        container.style.left = left + 'px';\n408\t        container.style.top = top + 'px';\n409\t    }\n410\t\n411\t    /**\n412\t     * Close context menu\n413\t     */\n414\t    function closeContextMenu() {\n415\t        const menu = document.getElementById('context-menu');\n416\t        if (menu) {\n417\t            menu.classList.remove('visible');\n418\t            delete menu.dataset.target;\n419\t        }\n420\t\n421\t        activeTarget = null;\n422\t        contextMenu null;\n427\t            if (controls) {\n428\t                controls.enabled = true;\n429\t            }\n430\t        }\n431\t\n432\t        // Remove Escape key handler\n433\t        teardownEscapeKeyHandler();\n434\t    }\n435\t\n436\t    /**\n437\t     * Set up Escape key handler for dismissing context menu\n438\t     */\n439\t    let escapeKeyHandler = null;\n440\t\n441\t    function setupEscapeKeyHandler() {\n442\t        // Remove existing handler if any\n443\t        teardownEscapeKeyHandler();\n444\t\n445\t        escapeKeyHandler = function(event) {\n446\t            if (event.key === 'Escape') {\n447\t                closeContextMenu();\n448\t            }\n449\t        };\n450\t\n451\t        document.addEventListener('keydown', escapeKeyHandler);\n452\t    }\n453\t\n454\t    function teardownEscapeKeyHandler() {\n455\t        if (escapeKeyHandler) {\n456\t            document.removeEventListener('keydown', escapeKeyHandler);\n457\t ============================================\n464\t\n465\t    /**\n466\t     * Execute a context menu action\n467\t     */\n468\t    async function executeAction(actionId) {\n469\t        if (!activeTarget) {\n470\t            console.error('[Quick Actions] No active target');\n471\t            return;\n472\t        }\n473\t\n474\t        const { type, data } = activeTarget;\n475\t        const actions = ACTIONS[type] || [];\n476\t        const action = actions.find(a => a.id === actionId);\n477\t\n478\t        if (!action) {\n479\t            console.error('[Quick Actions] Unknown action:', actionId);\n480\t            return;\n481\t        }\n482\t\n483\t        console.log('[Quick Actions] Executing:', actionId, 'on', type, data);\n484\t\n485\t        try {\n486\t            await action.action(data);\n487\t            showToast(`${action.label} executed`, 'info');\n488\t        } catch (error) {\n489\t            console.error('[Quick Actions] Action error:', error);\n490\t            showToast(`Action failed: ${error.message}`, 'warning');\n491\t        }\n492\t    }\n493\t\n494\t    // ============================================\n495\t    // Blob Actions\n496\t    // ============================================\n497\t\n498\t    function followBlob(blob) {\n499\t        if (window.Viz3D && window.Viz3D.setFollowTarget) {\n500\t            window.Viz3D.setFollowTarget(blob.id);\n501\t            showFollowIndicator(blob);\n502\t        } else {\n503\t            showToast('3D view not available', 'warning');\n504\t        }\n505\t    }\n506\t\n507\t    function showFollowIndicator(blob) {\n508\t        // Remove existing indicator\n509\t        if (followIndicator) {\n510\t            followIndicator.remove();\n511\t        }\n512\t\n513\t        // Create follow indicator\n514\t        followIndicator = document.createElement('div');\n515\t        followIndicator.className = 'follow-mode-indicator';\n516\t\n517\t        const personName = blob.person || 'Blob #' + blob.id;\n518\t        followIndicator.innerHTML = `\n519\t            <span>&#x1F50D;</span>\n520\t            <span>Following ${personName}</span>\n521\t            <button class=\"follow-stop-btn\" style=\"margin-left:12px;padding:4px 8px;border-radius:4px;border:none;background:rgba(255,255,255,0.2);color:white;cursor:pointer;\">Stop</button>\n522\t        `;\n523\t\n524\t        // Set up stop button handler\n525\t        const stopBtn = followIndicator.querySelector('.follow-stop-btn');\n526\t        if (stopBtn) {\n527\t            stopBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {\n528\t                stopFollowing();\n529\t            });\n530\t        }\n531\t\n532\t        document.body.appendChild(followIndicator);\n533\t\n534\t        // Set up scroll wheel zoom handler for follow mode\n535\t        setupFollowZoomHandler();\n536\t\n537\t        // Also set up ESC key to stop following\n538\t        document.addEventListener('keydown', handleFollowEscape);\n539\t    }\n540\t\n541\t    /**\n542\t     * Set up scroll wheel zoom handler for follow mode\n543\t     * Allows zoom adjustment while in follow mode\n544\t     */\n545\t    let followZoomHandler = null;\n546\t\n547\t    function setupFollowZoomHandler() {\n548\t        // Remove existing handler if any\n549\t        teardownFollowZoomHandler();\n550\t\n551\t        followZoomHandler = function(event) {\n552\t            if (!window.Viz3D) return;\n553\t\n554\t            const controls = window.Viz3D.controls ? window.Viz3D.controls() : null;\n555\t            if (!controls) return;\n556\t\n557\t            // Adjust zoom by changing camera distance\n558\t            // Positive delta (scroll up) = zoom in, Negative delta (scroll down) = zoom out\n559\t            const zoomSpeed = 0.001;\n560\t            const zoomFactor = Math.exp(-event.deltaY * zoomSpeed);\n561\t\n562\t            // Get current camera position relative to target\n563\t            const currentDistance = controls.object.position.distanceTo(controls.target);\n564\t\n565\t            // Apply zoom factor with limits\n566\t            const minDistance = 2;  // Minimum 2 meters from target\n567\t            const maxDistance = 20; // Maximum 20 meters from target\n568\t            const newDistance = Math.max(minDistance, Math.min(maxDistance, currentDistance * zoomFactor));\n569\t\n570\t            // Calculate new camera position along the same direction\n571\t            const direction = new THREE.Vector3();\n572\t            controls.object.position.sub(controls.target).normalize().multiplyScalar(newDistance).add(controls.target);\n573\t\n574\t            controls.update();\n575\t        };\n576\t\n577\t        // Attach to canvas\n578\t        const canvas = document.querySelector('#viz-canvas');\n579\t        if (canvas) {\n580\t            canvas.addEventListener('wheel', followZoomHandler, { passive: false });\n581\t        }\n582\t    }\n583\t\n584\t    function teardownFollowZoomHandler() {\n585\t        if (followZoomHandler) {\n586\t            const canvas = document.querySelector('#viz-canvas');\n587\t            if (canvas) {\n588\t                canvas.removeEventListener('wheel', followZoomHandler);\n589\t            }\n590\t            followZoomHandler = null;\n591\t        }\n592\t    }\n593\t\n594\t    function handleFollowEscape(e) {\n595\t        if (e.key === 'Escape') {\n596\t            stopFollowing();\n597\t        }\n598\t    }\n599\t\n600\t    function stopFollowing() {\n601\t        if (window.Viz3D && window.Viz3D.setFollowTarget) {\n602\t            window.Viz3D.setFollowTarget(null);\n603\t        }\n604\t        if (followIndicator) {\n605\t            followIndicator.remove();\n606\t            followIndicator = null;\n607\t        }\n608\t        document.removeEventListener('keydown', handleFollowEscape);\n609\t\n610\t        // Clean up zoom handler\n611\t        teardownFollowZoomHandler();\n612\t    }\n613\t\n614\t    function explainBlob(blob) {\n615\t        if       }\n620\t    }\n621\t\n622\t    function identifyPerson(blob) {\n623\t        // Open BLE panel to assign person\n624\t        if (window.BLEPanel) {\n625\t }\n701\t    }\n702\t\n703\t    // ============================================\n704\t    // Node Actions\n705\t    // ============================================\n706\t\n707\t    function confirmed;\n747\t        if (isLastOnline) {\n748\t            confirmed = confirm(\n749\t                `WARNING: ${node.name || node.mac} is the last online node!\\n\\n` +\n750\t                `Updating firmware will temporarily disconnect this node.\\n` +\n751\t                `This may result in loss of detection coverage.\\n\\n` +\n752\t                `Continue with OTA update?`\n753\t            );\n754\t        } else {\n755\t            confirmed = confirm(`Update firmware for ${node.name || node.mac}?`);\n756\t        }\n757\t\n758\t        if (!confirmed) return;\n759\t\n760\t        try {\n761\t            const response = await fetch(`/api/nodes/${node.mac}/update`, {\n762\t                method: 'POST'\n763\t            });\n764\t\n765\t            if (response.ok) {\n766\t                showToast(`Updating ${node.name || node.mac}`, 'info');\n767\t            } else {\n768\t                showToast('Failed to start update', 'warning');\n769\t            }\n770\t        } catch (error) {\n771\t            console.error('[Quick Actions] Error updating node:', error);\n772\t            showToast('Failed to start update', 'warning');\n773\t }\n1272\t\n1273\t    /**\n1274\t     * Initialize raycaster for right-click detection\n1275\t     */\n1276\t    function initializeRaycaster() {\n1277\t        if (!window.Viz3D) {\n1278\t            console.error('[Quick Actions] Viz3D not available');\n1279\t            return;\n1280\t        }\n1281\t\n1282\t        const raycaster = new THREE.Raycaster();\n1283\t        const mouse = new THREE.Vector2();\n1284\t\n1285\t        // Right-click handler on the canvas\n1286\t        document.addEventListener('contextmenu', function(event) {\n1287\t            // Only handle right-clicks on the canvas\n1288\t            const canvas = document.querySelector('#viz-canvas');\n1289\t            if (!canvas || !canvas.contains(event.target)) {\n1290\t                return;\n1291\t            }\n1292\t\n1293\t            event.preventDefault();\n1294\t            event.stopPropagation();\n1295\t\n1296\t            // If menu is already open, close it and return\n1297\t            if (contextMenu && contextMenu.classList.contains('visible')) {\n1298\t                closeContextMenu();\n1299\t                return;\n1300\t            }\n1301\t\n1302\t            // Get mouse position\n1303\t            const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();\n1304\t            mouse.x = ((event.clientX - rect.left) / rect.width) * 2 - 1;\n1305\t            mouse.y = -((event.clientY - rect.top) / rect.height) * 2 + 1;\n1306\t\n1307\t            // Get camera and scene from Viz3D\n1308\t            const camera = window.Viz3D.camera ? window.Viz3D.camera() : null;\n1309\t            const scene = window.Viz3D.scene ? window.Viz3D.scene() : null;\n1310\t\n1311\t            if (!camera || !scene) {\n1312\t                console.warn('[Quick Actions] Camera or scene not available');\n1313\t                return;\n1314\t            }\n1315\t\n1316\t            // Raycast\n1317\t            raycaster.setFromCamera(mouse, camera);\n1318\t\n1319\t            // Priority order: 1. Track blobs, 2. Node spheres, 3. Zone cuboids, 4. Portal planes, 5. Trigger volumes, 6. Ground plane\n1320\t\n1321\t            // Check for blob intersections (highest priority - users click on people most often)\n1322\t            const blobMeshes = window.Viz3D.blobMeshes ? window.Viz3D.blobMeshes() : [];\n1323\t            if (blobMeshes && blobMeshes.length > 0) {\n1324\t                const blobIntersects = raycaster.intersectObjects(blobMeshes, true);\n1325\t                if (blobIntersects.length > 0) {\n1326\t                    // Find the object with blobId in userData\n1327\t                    for (let i = 0; i < blobIntersects.length; i++) {\n1328\t                        let obj = blobIntersects[i].object;\n1329\t                        // Walk up parent chain to find group with blobId\n1330\t                        while (obj) {\n1331\t                            if (obj.userData && obj.userData.blobId) {\n1332\t                                const blob = findBlobById(obj.userData.blobId);\n1333\t                                if (blob) {\n1334\t                                    showContextMenu(event.clientX, event.clientY, 'blob', blob);\n1335\t                                    return;\n1336\t                                }\n1337\t                            }\n1338\t                            obj = obj.parent;\n1339\t                        }\n1340\t                    }\n1341\t                }\n1342\t            }\n1343\t\n1344\t            // Check for node intersections\n1345\t            const nodeMeshes = window.Viz3D.nodeMeshes ? window.Viz3D.nodeMeshes() : [];\n1346\t            if (nodeMeshes && nodeMeshes.length > 0) {\n1347\t                const nodeIntersects = raycaster.intersectObjects(nodeMeshes, true);\n1348\t                if (nodeIntersects.length > 0) {\n1349\t                    // Find the object with mac in userData\n1350\t                    for (let i = 0; i < nodeIntersects.length; i++) {\n1351\t                        let obj = nodeIntersects[i].object;\n1352\t              description: 'Place a virtual node at this position',\n                action: (pos) => addVirtualNode(pos)\n            },\n            {\n                id: 'create-zone',\n                label: 'Create zone here',\n                icon: '&#x26F6;',\n                description: 'Start zone creation mode',\n                action: (pos) => createZoneHere(pos)\n            },\n            {\n                id: 'set-home',\n                label: 'Set as home point',\n                icon: '&#x1F3E0;',\n                description: 'Set coordinate origin to this position',\n                action: (pos) => setHomeAsPoint(pos)\n            },\n            {\n                id: 'place-portal',\n                label: 'Place portal here',\n                icon: '&#x1F6AA;',\n                description: 'Start portal creation mode',\n                action: (pos) => placePortalHere(pos)\n            }\n        ],\n        portal: [\n            {\n                id: 'edit',\n                label: 'Edit portal',\n                icon: '&#x270F;',\n                description: 'Enter portal edit mode',\n                action: (portal) => editPortal(portal)\n            },\n            {\n                id: 'crossings',\n                label: 'View crossing history',\n                icon: '&#x1F4C5;',\n                description: 'View recent crossings',\n                action: (portal) => showPortalCrossings(portal)\n            },\n            { divider: true },\n            {\n                id: 'delete',\n                label: 'Delete portal',\n                icon: '&#x1F5D1;',\n                description: 'Remove this portal',\n                action: (portal) => deletePortal(portal)\n            }\n        ],\n        trigger: [\n            {\n                id: 'edit',\n                label: 'Edit trigger',\n                icon: '&#x270F;',\n                description: 'Open automation in builder',\n                action: (trigger) => editTrigger(trigger)\n            },\n            {\n                id: 'test',\n                label: 'Test fire',\n                icon: '&#x1F4AF;',\n                description: 'Fire automation with test_mode=true',\n                action: (trigger) => testTrigger(trigger)\n            },\n            {\n                id: 'toggle',\n                label: 'Enable / Disable',\n                icon: '&#x1F6AB;',\n                description: 'Toggle automation enabled state',\n                action: (trigger) => toggleTrigger(trigger)\n            },\n            { divider: true },\n            {\n                id: 'delete',\n                label: 'Delete trigger volume',\n                icon: '&#x1F5D1;',\n                description: 'Delete volume and associated trigger',\n                action: (trigger) => deleteTrigger(trigger)\n            }\n        ]\n    };\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Context Menu UI\n    // ============================================\n\n    /**\n     * Create context menu\n     */\n    function createContextMenu() {\n        if (document.getElementById('context-menu')) {\n            return;\n        }\n\n        const menu = document.createElement('div');\n        menu.id = 'context-menu';\n        menu.className = 'context-menu';\n        menu.innerHTML = `\n            <div class=\"context-backdrop\"></div>\n            <div class=\"context-container\">\n                <div class=\"context-header\">\n                    <span class=\"context-icon\" id=\"context-icon\">&#x2699;</span>\n                    <span class=\"context-title\" id=\"context-title\">Actions</span>\n                </div>\n                <div class=\"context-body\" id=\"context-body\">\n                    <!-- Actions will be populated dynamically -->\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        `;\n\n        document.body.appendChild(menu);\n\n        // Set up event listeners\n        const backdrop = menu.querySelector('.context-backdrop');\n        backdrop.addEventListener('click', closeContextMenu);\n\n        console.log('[Quick Actions] Context menu created');\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Show context menu\n     */\n    function showContextMenu(x, y, targetType, target) {\n        createContextMenu();\n\n        const menu = document.getElementById('context-menu');\n        const iconEl = document.getElementById('context-icon');\n        const titleEl = document.getElementById('context-title');\n        const bodyEl = document.getElementById('context-body');\n\n        if (!menu) return;\n\n        // Store target\n        activeTarget = { type: targetType, data: target };\n        contextMenu = menu;\n\n        // Set title based on target type\n        const titles = {\n            blob: target.person ? `${target.person}` : 'Person',\n            node: target.name || target.mac,\n            zone: target.name,\n            empty: 'Location',\n            portal: target.name,\n            trigger: target.name\n        };\n\n        titleEl.textContent = titles[targetType] || 'Actions';\n\n        // Set icon\n        const icons = {\n            blob: '&#x1F464;',\n            node: '&#x1F4F1;',\n            zone: '&#x1F3E0;',\n            empty: '&#x1F30E;',\n            portal: '&#x1F6AA;',\n            trigger: '&#x2699;'\n        };\n        iconEl.innerHTML = icons[targetType] || '&#x2699;';\n\n        // Populate actions (including dividers)\n        const actions = ACTIONS[targetType] || [];\n        let actionHTML = '';\n        actions.forEach(action => {\n            if (action.divider) {\n                actionHTML += '<div class=\"context-divider\"></div>';\n            } else {\n                actionHTML += `\n                    <div class=\"context-item\" data-action-id=\"${action.id}\">\n                        <span class=\"item-icon\">${action.icon}</span>\n                        <div class=\"item-content\">\n                            <div class=\"item-label\">${action.label}</div>\n                            <div class=\"item-description\">${action.description}</div>\n                        </div>\n                    </div>\n                `;\n            }\n        });\n        bodyEl.innerHTML = actionHTML;\n\n        // Position menu\n        positionMenu(x, y);\n\n        // Set target type on menu for styling\n        menu.dataset.target = targetType;\n\n        // Show menu\n        menu.classList.add('visible');\n\n        // Disable OrbitControls while menu is open\n        if (window.Viz3D) {\n            const controls = window.Viz3D.controls ? window.Viz3D.controls() : null;\n            if (controls) {\n                controls.enabled = false;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Set up action listeners (only for non-divider items)\n        bodyEl.querySelectorAll('.context-item').forEach(item => {\n            item.addEventListener('click', () => {\n                executeAction(item.dataset.actionId);\n                closeContextMenu();\n            });\n        });\n\n        // Set up Escape key to dismiss\n        setupEscapeKeyHandler();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Position context menu intelligently\n     */\n    function positionMenu(x, y) {\n        const menu = document.getElementById('context-menu');\n        if (!menu) return;\n\n        const container = menu.querySelector('.context-container');\n        const viewportWidth = window.innerWidth;\n        const viewportHeight = window.innerHeight;\n\n        // Get container dimensions\n        const rect = container.getBoundingClientRect();\n        const width = rect.width || 300;\n        const height = rect.height || 400;\n\n        // Calculate position (keep within viewport)\n        let left = x + 10;\n        let top = y + 10;\n\n        // Adjust if off-screen\n        if (left + width > viewportWidth) {\n            left = x - width - 10;\n        }\n\n        if (top + height > viewportHeight) {\n            top = y - height - 10;\n        }\n\n        // Ensure minimum margins\n        left = Math.max(10, Math.min(left, viewportWidth - width - 10));\n        top = Math.max(10, Math.min(top, viewportHeight - height - 10));\n\n        container.style.left = left + 'px';\n        container.style.top = top + 'px';\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Close context menu\n     */\n    function closeContextMenu() {\n        const menu = document.getElementById('context-menu');\n        if (menu) {\n            menu.classList.remove('visible');\n            delete menu.dataset.target;\n        }\n\n        activeTarget = null;\n        contextMenu = null;\n\n        // Re-enable OrbitControls when menu closes\n        if (window.Viz3D) {\n            const controls = window.Viz3D.controls ? window.Viz3D.controls() : null;\n            if (controls) {\n                controls.enabled = true;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Remove Escape key handler\n        teardownEscapeKeyHandler();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Set up Escape key handler for dismissing context menu\n     */\n    let escapeKeyHandler = null;\n\n    function setupEscapeKeyHandler() {\n        // Remove existing handler if any\n        teardownEscapeKeyHandler();\n\n        escapeKeyHandler = function(event) {\n            if (event.key === 'Escape') {\n                closeContextMenu();\n            }\n        };\n\n        document.addEventListener('keydown', escapeKeyHandler);\n    }\n\n    function teardownEscapeKeyHandler() {\n        if (escapeKeyHandler) {\n            document.removeEventListener('keydown', escapeKeyHandler);\n            escapeKeyHandler = null;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Action Execution\n    // ============================================\n\n    /**\n     * Execute a context menu action\n     */\n    async function executeAction(actionId) {\n        if (!activeTarget) {\n            console.error('[Quick Actions] No active target');\n            return;\n        }\n\n        const { type, data } = activeTarget;\n        const actions = ACTIONS[type] || [];\n        const action = actions.find(a => a.id === actionId);\n\n        if (!action) {\n            console.error('[Quick Actions] Unknown action:', actionId);\n            return;\n        }\n\n        console.log('[Quick Actions] Executing:', actionId, 'on', type, data);\n\n        try {\n            await action.action(data);\n            showToast(`${action.label} executed`, 'info');\n        } catch (error) {\n            console.error('[Quick Actions] Action error:', error);\n            showToast(`Action failed: ${error.message}`, 'warning');\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Blob Actions\n    // ============================================\n\n    function followBlob(blob) {\n        if (window.Viz3D && window.Viz3D.setFollowTarget) {\n            window.Viz3D.setFollowTarget(blob.id);\n            showFollowIndicator(blob);\n        } else {\n            showToast('3D view not available', 'warning');\n        }\n    }\n\n    function showFollowIndicator(blob) {\n        // Remove existing indicator\n        if (followIndicator) {\n            followIndicator.remove();\n        }\n\n        // Create follow indicator\n        followIndicator = document.createElement('div');\n        followIndicator.className = 'follow-mode-indicator';\n\n        const personName = blob.person || 'Blob #' + blob.id;\n        followIndicator.innerHTML = `\n            <span>&#x1F50D;</span>\n            <span>Following ${personName}</span>\n            <button class=\"follow-stop-btn\" style=\"margin-left:12px;padding:4px 8px;border-radius:4px;border:none;background:rgba(255,255,255,0.2);color:white;cursor:pointer;\">Stop</button>\n        `;\n\n        // Set up stop button handler\n        const stopBtn = followIndicator.querySelector('.follow-stop-btn');\n        if (stopBtn) {\n            stopBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {\n                stopFollowing();\n            });\n        }\n\n        document.body.appendChild(followIndicator);\n\n        // Set up scroll wheel zoom handler for follow mode\n        setupFollowZoomHandler();\n\n        // Also set up ESC key to stop following\n        document.addEventListener('keydown', handleFollowEscape);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Set up scroll wheel zoom handler for follow mode\n     * Allows zoom adjustment while in follow mode\n     */\n    let followZoomHandler = null;\n\n    function setupFollowZoomHandler() {\n        // Remove existing handler if any\n        teardownFollowZoomHandler();\n\n        followZoomHandler = function(event) {\n            if (!window.Viz3D) return;\n\n            const controls = window.Viz3D.controls ? window.Viz3D.controls() : null;\n            if (!controls) return;\n\n            // Adjust zoom by changing camera distance\n            // Positive delta (scroll up) = zoom in, Negative delta (scroll down) = zoom out\n            const zoomSpeed = 0.001;\n            const zoomFactor = Math.exp(-event.deltaY * zoomSpeed);\n\n            // Get current camera position relative to target\n            const currentDistance = controls.object.position.distanceTo(controls.target);\n\n            // Apply zoom factor with limits\n            const minDistance = 2;  // Minimum 2 meters from target\n            const maxDistance = 20; // Maximum 20 meters from target\n            const newDistance = Math.max(minDistance, Math.min(maxDistance, currentDistance * zoomFactor));\n\n            // Calculate new camera position along the same direction\n            const direction = new THREE.Vector3();\n            controls.object.position.sub(controls.target).normalize().multiplyScalar(newDistance).add(controls.target);\n\n            controls.update();\n        };\n\n        // Attach to canvas\n        const canvas = document.querySelector('#viz-canvas');\n        if (canvas) {\n            canvas.addEventListener('wheel', followZoomHandler, { passive: false });\n        }\n    }\n\n    function teardownFollowZoomHandler() {\n        if (followZoomHandler) {\n            const canvas = document.querySelector('#viz-canvas');\n            if (canvas) {\n                canvas.removeEventListener('wheel', followZoomHandler);\n            }\n            followZoomHandler = null;\n        }\n    }\n\n    function handleFollowEscape(e) {\n        if (e.key === 'Escape') {\n            stopFollowing();\n        }\n    }\n\n    function stopFollowing() {\n        if (window.Viz3D && window.Viz3D.setFollowTarget) {\n            window.Viz3D.setFollowTarget(null);\n        }\n        if (followIndicator) {\n            followIndicator.remove();\n            followIndicator = null;\n        }\n        document.removeEventListener('keydown', handleFollowEscape);\n\n        // Clean up zoom handler\n        teardownFollowZoomHandler();\n    }\n\n    function explainBlob(blob) {\n        if (window.ExplainabilityPanel) {\n            window.ExplainabilityPanel.showForBlob(blob.id);\n        } else {\n            showToast('Explainability not available', 'warning');\n        }\n    }\n\n    function identifyPerson(blob) {\n        // Open BLE panel to assign person\n        if (window.BLEPanel) {\n            window.BLEPanel.open();\n            // Highlight this blob in the panel\n            setTimeout(() => {\n                const blobEl = document.querySelector(`[data-blob-id=\"${blob.id}\"]`);\n                if (blobEl) {\n                    blobEl.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });\n                    blobEl.classList.add('highlight');\n                }\n            }, 100);\n        }\n    }\n\n    function markIncorrect(blob) {\n        if (window.FeedbackPanel) {\n            window.FeedbackPanel.markIncorrect(blob.id);\n        } else {\n            // Send feedback directly\n            fetch('/api/feedback', {\n                method: 'POST',\n                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n                body: JSON.stringify({\n                    type: 'incorrect',\n                    blob_id: blob.id,\n                    timestamp: Date.now()\n                })\n            }).then(() => {\n                showToast('Marked as incorrect. System will learn from this.', 'info');\n            });\n        }\n    }\n\n    function showBlobHistory(blob) {\n        // Navigate to timeline and filter for this blob/person\n        if (window.SpaxelRouter) {\n            window.SpaxelRouter.navigate('timeline');\n        }\n\n        // Set filter to this person\n        setTimeout(() => {\n            const filterSelect = document.getElementById('timeline-filter-person');\n            if (filterSelect && blob.person) {\n                // Add option if not exists\n                let option = filterSelect.querySelector(`option[value=\"${blob.person}\"]`);\n                if (!option) {\n                    option = document.createElement('option');\n                    option.value = blob.person;\n                    option.textContent = blob.person;\n                    filterSelect.appendChild(option);\n                }\n                filterSelect.value = blob.person;\n\n                // Trigger filter\n                filterSelect.dispatchEvent(new Event('change'));\n            }\n        }, 100);\n    }\n\n    function createPersonAutomation(blob) {\n        if (window.AutomationBuilder) {\n            window.AutomationBuilder.createNewForPerson(blob);\n        } else {\n            showToast('Automation builder not available', 'warning');\n        }\n    }\n\n    function setBlobUnknown(blob) {\n        // Remove identity assignment from this blob\n        if (window.SpaxelState) {\n            const blobs = window.SpaxelState.get('blobs');\n            if (blobs && blobs[blob.id]) {\n                blobs[blob.id].person = null;\n                blobs[blob.id].ble_device = null;\n                window.SpaxelState.set('blobs', blob.id, blobs[blob.id]);\n                showToast(`Set blob #${blob.id} as unknown`, 'info');\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Node Actions\n    // ============================================\n\n    function showNodeDiagnostics(node) {\n        if (window.LinkHealthPanel) {\n            window.LinkHealthPanel.showForNode(node.mac);\n        } else {\n            showToast('Link health panel not available', 'warning');\n        }\n    }\n\n    async function blinkNodeLED(node) {\n        try {\n            const response = await fetch(`/api/nodes/${node.mac}/identify`, {\n                method: 'POST'\n            });\n\n            if (response.ok) {\n                showToast(`Blinking ${node.name || node.mac}`, 'info');\n            } else {\n                showToast('Failed to blink LED', 'warning');\n            }\n        } catch (error) {\n            console.error('[Quick Actions] Error blinking LED:', error);\n            showToast('Failed to blink LED', 'warning');\n        }\n    }\n\n    function repositionNode(node) {\n        if (window.Placement) {\n            window.Placement.selectNode(node.mac);\n            // Switch to live view if not already\n            if (window.SpaxelRouter && window.SpaxelRouter.getMode() !== 'live') {\n                window.SpaxelRouter.navigate('live');\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    async function updateNodeFirmware(node) {\n        // Check if this is the last online node\n        const isLastOnline = node.isLastOnline || checkIfLastOnline(node);\n\n        let confirmed;\n        if (isLastOnline) {\n            confirmed = confirm(\n                `WARNING: ${node.name || node.mac} is the last online node!\\n\\n` +\n                `Updating firmware will temporarily disconnect this node.\\n` +\n                `This may result in loss of detection coverage.\\n\\n` +\n                `Continue with OTA update?`\n            );\n        } else {\n            confirmed = confirm(`Update firmware for ${node.name || node.mac}?`);\n        }\n\n        if (!confirmed) return;\n\n        try {\n            const response = await fetch(`/api/nodes/${node.mac}/update`, {\n                method: 'POST'\n            });\n\n            if (response.ok) {\n                showToast(`Updating ${node.name || node.mac}`, 'info');\n            } else {\n                showToast('Failed to start update', 'warning');\n            }\n        } catch (error) {\n            console.error('[Quick Actions] Error updating node:', error);\n            showToast('Failed to start update', 'warning');\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Check if a node is the last online node\n     */\n    function checkIfLastOnline(node) {\n        if (!node || !node.mac) return false;\n\n        if (window.SpaxelState) {\n            const nodes = window.SpaxelState.get('nodes');\n            if (!nodes) return false;\n\n            let onlineCount = 0;\n            for (let mac in nodes) {\n                const n = nodes[mac];\n                if (n && n.status === 'online') {\n                    onlineCount++;\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Check if this is the only online node\n            return onlineCount === 1 && nodes[node.mac] && nodes[node.mac].status === 'online';\n        }\n\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    function showNodeLinks(node) {\n        if (window.Viz3D && window.Viz3D.highlightNodeLinks) {\n            // Clear any existing highlights first\n            window.Viz3D.clearLinkHighlights();\n            // Highlight links for this node\n            window.Viz3D.highlightNodeLinks(node.mac, true, 0x4fc3f7);\n            showToast('Links highlighted. Click elsewhere to clear.', 'info');\n\n            // Auto-clear after 5 seconds\n            setTimeout(function() {\n                if (window.Viz3D && window.Viz3D.clearLinkHighlights) {\n                    window.Viz3D.clearLinkHighlights();\n                }\n            }, 5000);\n        }\n    }\n\n    async function disableNode(node) {\n        const confirmed = confirm(`Disable ${node.name || node.mac}?`);\n        if (!confirmed) return;\n\n        try {\n            const response = await fetch(`/api/nodes/${node.mac}/disable`, {\n                method: 'POST'\n            });\n\n            if (response.ok) {\n                showToast(`${node.name || node.mac} disabled`, 'info');\n            } else {\n                showToast('Failed to disable node', 'warning');\n            }\n        } catch (error) {\n            console.error('[Quick Actions] Error disabling node:', error);\n            showToast('Failed to disable node', 'warning');\n        }\n    }\n\n    function removeNode(node) {\n        const confirmed = confirm(`Remove ${node.name || node.mac} from the fleet?`);\n        if (!confirmed) return;\n\n        // This would normally open a confirmation dialog in the UI\n        showToast('Node removal requires confirmation in Fleet panel', 'info');\n    }\n\n    function editNodeLabel(node) {\n        // Open inline edit field for node label\n        const newName = prompt(`Enter new name for ${node.name || node.mac}:`, node.name || '');\n        if (newName === null) return; // User cancelled\n        if (newName.trim() === '') {\n            showToast('Name cannot be empty', 'warning');\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Update node name via API\n        fetch(`/api/nodes/${node.mac}`, {\n            method: 'PATCH',\n            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n            body: JSON.stringify({ name: newName.trim() })\n        })\n        .then(response => {\n            if (response.ok) {\n                showToast(`Node renamed to \"${newName.trim()}\"`, 'info');\n                // Update state if available\n                if (window.SpaxelState) {\n                    const nodes = window.SpaxelState.get('nodes');\n                    if (nodes && nodes[node.mac]) {\n                        nodes[node.mac].name = newName.trim();\n                        window.SpaxelState.set('nodes', node.mac, nodes[node.mac]);\n                    }\n                }\n            } else {\n                showToast('Failed to rename node', 'warning');\n            }\n        })\n        .catch(error => {\n            console.error('[Quick Actions] Error renaming node:', error);\n            showToast('Failed to rename node', 'warning');\n        });\n    }\n\n    function reassignNodeRole(node) {\n        // Open role picker dialog\n        const roles = ['tx', 'rx', 'tx_rx', 'passive', 'idle'];\n        const roleLabels = {\n            'tx': 'TX (Transmitter only)',\n            'rx': 'RX (Receiver only)',\n            'tx_rx': 'TX/RX (Both)',\n            'passive': 'Passive (RX from router)',\n            'idle': 'Idle (Disabled)'\n        };\n\n        const currentRole = node.role || 'tx_rx';\n        let message = 'Select new role for ' + (node.name || node.mac) + ':\\n\\n';\n        roles.forEach((r, i) => {\n            message += `${i + 1}. ${roleLabels[r]}${r === currentRole ? ' (current)' : ''}\\n`;\n        });\n        message += '\\nEnter number (1-' + roles.length + '):';\n\n        const choice = prompt(message);\n        if (choice === null) return; // User cancelled\n\n        const choiceNum = parseInt(choice, 10);\n        if (isNaN(choiceNum) || choiceNum < 1 || choiceNum > roles.length) {\n            showToast('Invalid choice', 'warning');\n            return;\n        }\n\n        const newRole = roles[choiceNum - 1];\n        if (newRole === currentRole) {\n            showToast('Role unchanged', 'info');\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Update node role via API\n        fetch(`/api/nodes/${node.mac}`, {\n            method: 'PATCH',\n            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n            body: JSON.stringify({ role: newRole })\n        })\n        .then(response => {\n            if (response.ok) {\n                showToast(`Role changed to ${roleLabels[newRole]}`, 'info');\n                // Update state if available\n                if (window.SpaxelState) {\n                    const nodes = window.SpaxelState.get('nodes');\n                    if (nodes && nodes[node.mac]) {\n                        nodes[node.mac].role = newRole;\n                        window.SpaxelState.set('nodes', node.mac, nodes[node.mac]);\n                    }\n                }\n            } else {\n                showToast('Failed to change role', 'warning');\n            }\n        })\n        .catch(error => {\n            console.error('[Quick Actions] Error changing role:', error);\n            showToast('Failed to change role', 'warning');\n        });\n    }\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Zone Actions\n    // ============================================\n\n    function showZoneHistory(zone) {\n        // Navigate to timeline and filter for this zone\n        if (window.SpaxelRouter) {\n            window.SpaxelRouter.navigate('timeline');\n        }\n\n        setTimeout(() => {\n            const filterSelect = document.getElementById('timeline-filter-zone');\n            if (filterSelect) {\n                // Add option if not exists\n                let option = filterSelect.querySelector(`option[value=\"${zone.name}\"]`);\n                if (!option) {\n                    option = document.createElement('option');\n                    option.value = zone.name;\n                    option.textContent = zone.name;\n                    filterSelect.appendChild(option);\n                }\n                filterSelect.value = zone.name;\n\n                // Trigger filter\n                filterSelect.dispatchEvent(new Event('change'));\n            }\n        }, 100);\n    }\n\n    function editZoneBounds(zone) {\n        if (window.Placement) {\n            window.Placement.editZone(zone.id);\n        }\n    }\n\n    function renameZone(zone) {\n        // Inline rename zone\n        const newName = prompt(`Enter new name for zone \"${zone.name}\":`, zone.name);\n        if (newName === null) return; // User cancelled\n        if (newName.trim() === '') {\n            showToast('Name cannot be empty', 'warning');\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Update zone name via API\n        fetch(`/api/zones/${zone.id}`, {\n            method: 'PATCH',\n            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n            body: JSON.stringify({ name: newName.trim() })\n        })\n        .then(response => {\n            if (response.ok) {\n                showToast(`Zone renamed to \"${newName.trim()}\"`, 'info');\n                // Update state if available\n                if (window.SpaxelState) {\n                    const zones = window.SpaxelState.get('zones');\n                    if (zones && zones[zone.id]) {\n                        zones[zone.id].name = newName.trim();\n                        window.SpaxelState.set('zones', zone.id, zones[zone.id]);\n                    }\n                }\n            } else {\n                showToast('Failed to rename zone', 'warning');\n            }\n        })\n        .catch(error => {\n            console.error('[Quick Actions] Error renaming zone:', error);\n            showToast('Failed to rename zone', 'warning');\n        });\n    }\n\n    function createZoneAutomation(zone) {\n        if (window.AutomationBuilder) {\n            window.AutomationBuilder.createNewForZone(zone);\n        }\n    }\n\n    function showZoneCrowdFlow(zone) (longPressTimer) {\n                clearTimeout(longPressTimer);\n                longPressTimer = null;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    function handleTouchEnd() {\n        if Linear regression (OLS): fit `phase = a*k + b` over data subcarriers\n46\t  - STO/CFO removal: residual phase = unwrapped - (slope × k + intercept)\n47\t  - HT20 subcarrier map: 64 total, 46 data (excluding null, guard, pilot)\n48\t\n49\t- **Baseline system (`signal/baseline.go`):**\n50\t  - EMA baseline per link per subcarrier: `baseline = α×amplitude + (1-α)×baseline`\n51\t  - α = dt / (τ + dt) ≈ 0.0033 for dt=0.1s, τ=30s\n52\t  - Motion-gated updates: only update when smoothDeltaRMS < 0.05\n53\t  - Confidence scoring: 0.3 for stale baselines (>7 days), asymptotically → 1.0\n54\t  - Snapshot/restore for SQLite persistence\n55\t  - BaselineManager for multi-link coordination\n56\t\n57\t- **Motion detection (`signal/features.go`):**\n58\t  - NBVI (Normalized Bandwidth Variance Index): `Var(amp) / Mean(amp)²`\n59\t  - Welford's online algorithm for numerically stable variance\n60\t  - Top-16 subcarrier selection by NBVI score\n61\t  - deltaRMS: `sqrt(mean((amp - baseline)²))` over selected subcarriers\n62\t  - Exponential smoothing: `smooth = 0.3×raw + 0.7×prev`\n63\t  - Motion threshold: smoothDeltaRMS > 0.02\n64\t\n65\t- **Link processor (`signal/processor.go`):**\n66\t  - LinkProcessor: ties together phase sanitization, baseline, motion detection\n67\t  - ProcessorManager: manages per-link processors with thread-safe access\n68\t  - GetAllMotionStates(): returns motion state for all links\n69\t  - GetAllBaselines()/RestoreBaseline(): for SQLite persistence\n70\t\n71\t**Constants used (from plan):**\n72\t- RSSIRefdBm = -30.0\n73\t- DefaultMotionThreshold = 0.05\n74\t- DefaultDeltaRMSThreshold = 0.02\n75\t- NBVITopCount = 16\n76\t- NBVIMinThreshold = 0.001\n77\t- DeltaRMSSmoothingAlpha = 0.3\n78\t\n79\t**Tests:** 37 tests covering phase sanitization, baseline, NBVI, motion detection. All pass.\n80\t\n81\t**Files created:**\n82\t```\n83\tmothership/internal/signal/\n84\t├── phase.go          — Phase sanitization algorithms\n85\t├── phase_test.go     — 15 tests for phase processing\n86\t├── baseline.go       — EMA baseline management\n87\t├── baseline_test.go  — 9 tests for baseline\n88\t├── features.go       — NBVI selection, deltaRMS, motion detection\n89\t├── features_test.go  — 13 tests for features\n90\t└── processor.go      — LinkProcessor, ProcessorManager\n91\t```\n92\t\n93\t**Remaining for Phase 2:**\n94\t- Dashboard presence indicator\n95\t- CSI recording buffer\n96\t- Adaptive sensing rate\n97\t\n98\t#### Iteration 4 — 2026-03-26\n99\t\n100\t**Completed:** Docker packaging\n101\t\n102\tImplemented container deployment with:\n103\t\n104\t- **Dockerfile:** Multi-stage build for minimal production image\n105\t  - Complex CSI computation: int8 I/Q → float64 complex → amplitude/phase\n  - RSSI normalization (AGC compensation): `norm = 10^((rssi_ref - rssi)/20)`\n  - Spatial phase unwrapping: correct 2π jumps between adjacent subcarriers\n  - Linear regression (OLS): fit `phase = a*k + b` over data subcarriers\n  - STO/CFO removal: residual phase = unwrapped - (slope × k + intercept)\n  - HT20 subcarrier map: 64 total, 46 data (excluding null, guard, pilot)\n\n- **Baseline system (`signal/baseline.go`):**\n  - EMA baseline per link per subcarrier: `baseline = α×amplitude + (1-α)×baseline`\n  - α = dt / (τ + dt) ≈ 0.0033 for dt=0.1s, τ=30s\n  - Motion-gated updates: only update when smoothDeltaRMS < 0.05\n  - Confidence scoring: 0.3 for stale baselines (>7 days), asymptotically → 1.0\n  - Snapshot/restore for SQLite persistence\n  - BaselineManager for multi-link coordination\n\n- **Motion detection (`signal/features.go`):**\n  - NBVI (Normalized Bandwidth Variance Index): `Var(amp) / Mean(amp)²`\n  - Welford's online algorithm for numerically stable variance\n  - Top-16 subcarrier selection by NBVI score\n  - deltaRMS: `sqrt(mean((amp - baseline)²))` over selected subcarriers\n  - Exponential smoothing: `smooth = 0.3×raw + 0.7×prev`\n  - Motion threshold: smoothDeltaRMS > 0.02\n\n- **Link processor (`signal/processor.go`):**\n  - LinkProcessor: ties together phase sanitization, baseline, motion detection\n  - ProcessorManager: manages per-link processors with thread-safe access\n  - GetAllMotionStates(): returns motion state for all links\n  - GetAllBaselines()/RestoreBaseline(): for SQLite persistence\n\n**Constants used (from plan):**\n- RSSIRefdBm = -30.0\n- DefaultMotionThreshold = 0.05\n- DefaultDeltaRMSThreshold = 0.02\n- NBVITopCount = 16\n- NBVIMinThreshold = 0.001\n- DeltaRMSSmoothingAlpha = 0.3\n\n**Tests:** 37 tests covering phase sanitization, baseline, NBVI, motion detection. AccuracyTracker with rolling 7-day window\n\n**Phase 7 Status:** COMPLETE\n\n## Phase 8 — Analysis & Developer Tools\n\nGoal: Deep debugging, system tuning, and detection explainability.\n\n### Status: COMPLETE\n\n| Item | Status | Notes |\n|------|--------|-------|\n| Activity timeline (Component 27) | **Done** | Universal event stream with tap-to-time-travel |\n| Detection explainability buffered queue\n- Handles all event types: detections, zone transitions, alerts, system events, learning milestones\n- WebSocket push of new events to dashboard clients in real-time\n- REST API: `GET /api/events` with cursor-based pagination, filters (type/zone/person/time), and FTS5 search\n- Frontend: `sidebar-timeline.js` — virtualized list, tap-to-time-travel, inline feedback buttons\n\n**Detection explainability (`internal/explainability/`):**\n- `Handler` maintains per-blob explanation data updated by the fusion engine\n- Per-link contribution table: deltaRMS, Fresnel zone number, learned weight, contribution amount\n- BLE match details: per-node RSSI, triangulation position, confidence\n- Fresnel zone ellipsoid geometry for 3D visualization\n- Frontend: `explainability.js` — X-ray overlay dims non-contributors, glowing contributing links\n\n**Time-travel debugging (`internal/replay/`):**\n- Append-only `csi_replay.bin` with per-frame records (recv_time_ms + raw CSI binary)\n- `Worker` manages replay sessions: play/pause/seek/speed control\n- Parameter tuning: `PATCH /api/replay/params` re-runs pipeline on buffered data at max speed\n- \"Apply to Live\" copies tuned params to the running pipeline\n- Dashboard: timeline scrubber integrated with activity timeline events\n\n**Pre-deployment simulator (`internal/simulator/`):**\n- `Space` defines room geometry with wall segments and material properties\n- `NodeSet` manages virtual TX/RX node placement\n- `WalkerSet` simulates random-walk or path-following persons\n- Two-ray propagation model with path loss + wall penetration + first-order reflections\n- GDOP computation per cell using Fisher information matrix\n- REST API at `/api/simulator/*` for space/node/walker management and GDOP computation\n\n**CSI simulator CLI (`cmd/sim/`):**\n- Connects to mothership as virtual nodes, sends synthetic CSI binary frames\n- Walker random-walk model with Gaussian velocity updates, wall reflection\n- Amplitude/phase generated from propagation model with Gaussian noise injection\n- Optional BLE advertisement simulation (`--ble` flag)\n- Verified authentication (exits non-zero on `{type:\"reject\"}`)\n- Integration test support: polls `GET /api/blobs` for blob count assertions\n\n**Fresnel zone debug overlay (`dashboard/js/fresnel.js`):**\n- Toggle-able wireframe ellipsoids between active TX/RX link pairs\n- Ellipsoid geometry computed from TX/RX positions and Fresnel zone number\n- Color-coded by zone number (zone 1 = bright, outer zones = dimmer)\n- Toolbar button integration with existing layers panel\n\n**Files created/modified:**\n```\nmothership/internal/timeline/       — timeline.go, timeline_test.go, handler.go, per-user default stored in `localStorage`\n\n**Ambient dashboard (`dashboard/ambient.html`, `dashboard/js/ambient.js`):**\n- Served at `/ambient` — separate lightweight route for wall-mounted tablets\n- Canvas 2D renderer: colored circles for people, zone labels, soft glow effects\n- Time-of-day palette: morning (cool), day (neutral), evening (amber), night (very dim)\n- Auto-dim when house empty for 30+ min; gentle fade-in on person detection\n- Alert mode: pulsing red border + large text + action buttons on fall/security events\n- Morning briefing integration: briefing text shown on first detection, fades after 30 s\n- Reconnect backoff handles WebSocket drops gracefully\n\n**Spatial quick actions (`dashboard/js/quick-actions.js`):**\n- Three.js Raycaster determines target under cursor (person/node/zone/portal/trigger/empty)\n- Context menu component renders appropriate options per target type\n- Per-blob: \"Who is this?\", \"Why?\", \"Follow\" camera, \"Create automation\", \"Mark incorrect\"\n- Per-node: \"Diagnostics\", \"Blink LED\", \"Reposition\", \"Update firmware\", \"Show links\"\n- Per-empty: \"What happened here?\", \"Add trigger zone\", \"Add virtual node\", \"Coverage quality\"\n- Per-zone: \"Zone history\", \"Edit zone\", \"Create automation\", \"Crowd flow\"\n- \"Follow\" mode: camera smoothly tracks person, auto-orbiting to keep them centered\n\n**Command palette (`dashboard/js/command-palette.js`):**\n- Ctrl+K (Cmd+K on Mac) opens universal search and command interface\n- Fuzzy matching across zones, persons, nodes, settings, help topics, events\n- Navigate time: \"last night 2am\", \"yesterday kitchen\", \"this morning\"\n- Execute commands: \"update all nodes\", \"re-baseline kitchen\", \"arm security\"\n- Help: \"help fall detection\", \"why false positive\", \"troubleshoot kitchen\"\n- Recently used commands surface first; expert mode only\n\n**Morning briefing (`internal/briefing/`, `dashboard/js/briefing.js`):**\n- `Generator` assembles briefing in priority order from sleep, events, anomalies, system health\n- Priority blocks: critical alerts → sleep summary → who is home → overnight anomalies → system health → predictions → learning progress\n- Degenerate case: \"All quiet last night. All systems healthy.\"\n- Stored in `briefings` SQLite table (one per day per person)\n- REST API: `GET /api/briefing`, `GET /api/briefing/current`\n- Dashboard: card overlay on first open, dismissible, slides away after 10 s\n\n**Guided troubleshooting (`internal/guidedtroubleshoot/`, `dashboard/js/troubleshoot.js`):**\n- Trigger conditions: detection quality drops, repeated setting changes, node offline >2 h\n- Repeated-edit detection: per-key counter in memory; hint delivered in `GET /api/settings` response as `\"repeated_edit_hint\": true`\n- Proactive diagnostic flow: check connectivity → show link health → suggest repositioning → offer re-baseline\n- First-time feature tooltips shown once, dismissed on click, stored in `localStorage`\n- Post-feedback explanations in timeline after incorrect/missed detection feedback\n\n**Mobile-responsive expert mode (`dashboard/js/mobile.js` + CSS):**\n- Touch orbit (one finger), pan (two fingers), pinch-zoom (two fingers)\n- FXAA anti-aliasing replaces MSAA on mobile (better performance on low-power GPUs)\n- Hamburger menu for toolbar panels on small screens\n- Viewport meta tag with `viewport-fit=cover` for notch-aware layout\n- CSS Grid layout collapses gracefully on narrow viewports\n\n**Fleet status page (`dashboard/fleet.html`, `dashboard/js/fleet-page.js`):**\n- Full table with sortable columns: Name, MAC, Role, Position (fly-to), Firmware, RSSI, Status, Uptime, Actions\n- OTA progress bar per node during updates (PENDING → DOWNLOADING → REBOOTING → VERIFIED / FAILED)\n- Bulk actions: Update All (rolling OTA), Re-baseline All, Export Config, Import Config\n- Camera fly-to: clicking position coordinates in table jumps 3D camera to that node\n- Responsive layout works on both desktop and tablet\n\n**Files created/modified:**\n```\ndashboard/simple.html               — Simple mode page\ndashboard/ambient.html              — Ambient dashboard page\ndashboard/fleet.html                —
